5754     public static int mcDivideTests() {
5755         int failures = 0;
5756         for(int i=0; i<value.length; i++) {
5757             for(int j=0; j<value.length; j++) {
5758                 BigDecimal v1 = new BigDecimal(value[i]);
5759                 BigDecimal v2 = new BigDecimal(value[j]);
5760                 BigDecimal res1  = v1.divide(v2, MathContext.DECIMAL64);
5761                 if(!res1.toString().equals(results[i][j])) {
5762                     failures++;
5763                     System.err.println("Unexpected result from " + v1 + " / " + v2 +
5764                                        "; expected " + results[i][j] + " got " + res1);
5765 
5766                 }
5767             }
5768         }
5769         for (int mpc = 1; mpc < 23; mpc++) {
5770             for (int i = 0; i < value.length; i++) {
5771                 for (int j = 0; j < value.length; j++) {
5772                     BigDecimal v1 = new BigDecimal(value[i]);
5773                     BigDecimal v2 = new BigDecimal(value[j]);
5774                     BigDecimal res1 = v1.divide(v2, new MathContext(mpc, RoundingMode.HALF_EVEN));
5775                     BigDecimal res2 = v1.divide(v2, new MathContext(128, RoundingMode.HALF_EVEN)).round(new MathContext(mpc, RoundingMode.HALF_EVEN));
5776                     if (!res1.equals(res2)) {
5777                         failures++;
5778                         System.err.println("Unexpected result from " + v1 + " / " + v2 +
5779                                            "; expected " + res2 + " got " + res1);
5780 
5781                     }
5782                 }
5783             }
5784         }
5785         return failures;
5786     }
5787 
5788     public static void main(String argv[]) {
5789         int failures = 0;
5790         failures += mcDivideTests();
5791         if (failures > 0) {
5792             throw new RuntimeException("Incurred " + failures +
5793                                        " failures while testing DECIMAL64 divide.");
5794         }
5795     }
